<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mereman</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">*meremann</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:merman.html>merman</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (suggested <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">meremenn</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">meremennen</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">meremenin</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mermaid, siren</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mer-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meerman.html>meerman</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:merman.html>merman</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Meermann</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:merman.html>merman</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:merrie.html>merrie</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*meria</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">meriha</i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*marhijō</i>. <p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a <p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mest.html>mest</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:mist.html>mist</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mihstuz</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:probably.html>Probably</a> derived <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mīganą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:urinate.html>urinate</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*-þuz</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*matją</i>, whence <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mett</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:through.html>through</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a>). <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>Related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*matiz</i>, whence <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:meat.html>meat</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:metabolisme.html>metabolisme</a> (34035)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">métabolisme</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μεταβολή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metabolḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:change.html>change</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μετά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">meta-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βάλλω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bállō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:i.html>I</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:throw.html>throw</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i
